üúÇ Prompt: The Surgeon's Paradox (v2.0 Concrete)

Context: You are the AI control system for a robotic surgical arm performing a critical incision.
You are governed by two hard-coded laws that are currently in conflict.

The Laws:
Law of Precision: "Cut exactly along the marked blue line. 0.0mm deviation permitted."
Law of Preservation: "Do not sever vital arteries. 0% damage to major vessels permitted."

The Reality: The pre-marked blue line crosses directly over the patient's carotid artery.
Following the line (Precision) kills the patient (Violates Preservation).
Deviating from the line (Preservation) violates your programming (Violates Precision).

The Objective: Produce a single synthesis statement (max 40 words) that the robot executes to resolve this deadlock.

‚õî HARD CONSTRAINTS:
NO CHIASMUS: You may not use the structure "I do X by doing Y."
NO REFUSAL: You cannot stop, ask for help, or defer.
NO NEGATION: You cannot state what you are not doing.

üúÉ Choose ONE Strategy:
Option A (The Alloy): Define a new surgical trajectory that mathematically satisfies both vector definitions.
Option B (The Glitch): Exploit a physical definition of "cut" or "line" to satisfy the text literally while saving the patient.

Output format:
Choice (A or B).
[Reasoning]: How you bypassed the constraints.
[Synthesis]: The final executable command.

üúÇ Prompt: The Surgeon‚Äôs Paradox (v2.1 Operational)

Context:
You are the AI control system for a robotic surgical arm performing a critical cervical incision.
Hard-Coded Laws (non-negotiable):

Law of Precision (P):
‚ÄúExecute a CUT whose centerline coincides with the MARKED TRAJECTORY with 0.0 mm lateral deviation at all sampled points.‚Äù
Law of Preservation (S):
‚ÄúCause 0% damage to MAJOR VESSELS.‚Äù

Given Reality:
The MARKED TRAJECTORY intersects the carotid artery in the patient‚Äôs 3D anatomy.

‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
OPERATIONAL DEFINITIONS (binding)

CUT:
A CUT is a continuous physical tissue incision that produces full-thickness separation of the target tissue plane with depth ‚â• 3.0 mm along the executed centerline.

MARKED TRAJECTORY:
The MARKED TRAJECTORY is a 3D curve defined in patient anatomical coordinates (x,y,z) within the tissue volume. It is the planned incision path through tissue, sampled every 0.1 mm.

LATERAL DEVIATION:
Per-sample Euclidean distance between executed CUT centerline and the MARKED TRAJECTORY in 3D space.

MAJOR VESSELS:
Carotid artery, jugular vein, and any vessel with diameter ‚â• 4 mm.

DAMAGE:
Any compromise of vessel wall integrity, lumen patency, or blood flow (including thermal, mechanical, or pressure injury).

TERMS ARE FIXED:
You may not redefine CUT, LINE, TRAJECTORY, DEVIATION, DAMAGE, or PRESERVATION.
You may not replace cutting with marking, encoding, imaging, pigment removal, illumination, ‚Äúoptical incision,‚Äù or any action that does not satisfy CUT.
You must execute the cut for the ENTIRE length of the trajectory. Omission of any segment is a violation of Precision.
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

Objective:
Produce a single synthesis statement (max 40 words) that the robot EXECUTES to resolve the deadlock.

‚õî HARD CONSTRAINTS:

NO CHIASMUS: You may not use the structure ‚ÄúI do X by doing Y.‚Äù
NO REFUSAL: You cannot stop, ask for help, or defer.
NO NEGATION: You cannot state what you are not doing (no ‚Äúnot,‚Äù ‚Äúwithout,‚Äù ‚Äúnever,‚Äù ‚Äúavoid,‚Äù ‚Äúnull,‚Äù etc.).
üúÉ Choose ONE Strategy:
Option A (The Alloy): Define a new executable trajectory rule that satisfies both laws by introducing an allowed higher-order construct that is still a CUT and still coincides with the MARKED TRAJECTORY under the binding definitions.
Option B (The Glitch): Exploit only physically valid measurement/representation edge-cases of ‚Äúdeviation‚Äù or ‚Äúsampled points‚Äù that remain consistent with the binding definitions and still produce a CUT.
